
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Analyze the properties of the convex equilateral hexagon with opposite sides parallel to establish geometric relationships.'}, {'objective': "Express the directions and lengths of the hexagon's sides and their extensions to form the triangle with sides 200, 240, and 300."}, {'objective': 'Relate the side length of the hexagon to the side lengths of the triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF.'}, {'objective': "Use the triangle side lengths and geometric relations to set up equations involving the hexagon's side length."}, {'objective': 'Solve the equations to find the side length of the equilateral hexagon.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The figure is a convex equilateral hexagon ABCDEF.
- All pairs of opposite sides are parallel, implying AB || DE, BC || EF, and CD || FA.
- The hexagon is equilateral, so all its sides have the same length, which is unknown.
- A triangle is formed by the extensions of segments AB, CD, and EF.
- The triangle formed by these extended lines has side lengths 200, 240, and 300.
- The objective is to find the side length of the hexagon.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The hexagon’s opposite sides being parallel suggests it is a parallelogon (a polygon with pairs of parallel opposite sides), which imposes strong geometric constraints.
- Since the hexagon is equilateral and convex, all sides are equal in length and the interior angles are less than 180°.
- The triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF corresponds to the triangle formed by the intersection points of the lines containing these sides.
- The side lengths of this triangle (200, 240, 300) relate to the distances between these intersection points.
- The problem likely involves relating the side length of the hexagon to the dimensions of this triangle, possibly through vector or coordinate geometry or by using properties of parallelogons.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in Euclidean geometry, specifically polygon geometry.
- Subfields include convex polygons, properties of equilateral polygons, and line geometry (intersections and extensions).
- The problem may also involve vector methods or analytic geometry to relate side lengths and angles.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and advanced geometry studies.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The exact configuration of the hexagon (e.g., orientation, labeling) is not fully specified but can be inferred from the naming and parallelism.
- The nature of the triangle formed by the extensions: whether it is the triangle formed by the intersection points of the lines containing AB, CD, and EF, or another construction.
- Assumptions such as the hexagon being strictly convex and the order of vertices are implied but not explicitly stated.
- It may be necessary to assume standard orientation and labeling conventions to proceed.
- Potential challenges include relating the side length of the hexagon to the triangle side lengths without explicit angle measures.

============== code generate 0 ================
async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Formally represent the convex equilateral hexagon ABCDEF using vector notation or coordinate geometry. "
        "Define vectors for each side (AB, BC, CD, DE, EF, FA) and incorporate the given conditions: the hexagon is equilateral (all sides equal length) and convex, "
        "and opposite sides are parallel (AB || DE, BC || EF, CD || FA). Establish the relationships between these vectors, including parallelism and equality of magnitudes. "
        "Choose a convenient coordinate system to simplify the problem, such as placing vertex A at the origin and side AB along the x-axis."
    )
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, representing hexagon vectors, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking1,
        "answer": answer1
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2: Represent the triangle formed by the extensions of sides AB, CD, and EF. "
        "Identify the lines containing these sides and find their pairwise intersections to form the triangle. "
        "Express the side lengths of this triangle in terms of the vectors or parameters defined for the hexagon sides. "
        "Validate that the triangle formed by these intersections corresponds to the given side lengths 200, 240, and 300. "
        "Provide a detailed geometric or algebraic derivation relating the hexagon's side vectors to the triangle's side lengths."
    )
    cot_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content, answer1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent_2([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], cot_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2.id}, representing triangle from extended sides, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc2['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking2,
        "answer": answer2
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_3 = (
        "Sub-task 3: Using the vector or coordinate representations and relationships from previous subtasks, "
        "derive equations relating the hexagon's side length to the triangle's side lengths (200, 240, 300). "
        "Solve these equations to find the numerical value of the hexagon's side length. "
        "Use algebraic manipulation, properties of parallelogons, vector addition, and trigonometric laws as needed. "
        "Ensure the solution respects the convexity and equilateral conditions of the hexagon."
    )
    N = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_3 = []
    possible_thinkings_3 = []
    subtask_desc3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content, answer1.content, thinking2.content, answer2.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agents_3[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2], cot_sc_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_3[i].id}, deriving and solving equations for hexagon side length, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
        possible_answers_3.append(answer3)
        possible_thinkings_3.append(thinking3)

    final_instr_3 = "Given all the above thinking and answers, find the most consistent and correct solution for the hexagon's side length."
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo] + possible_answers_3 + possible_thinkings_3, "Sub-task 3: Synthesize and choose the most consistent answer for the hexagon side length." + final_instr_3, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, synthesizing consistent solution for hexagon side length, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc3['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking3,
        "answer": answer3
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_reflect_instruction_4 = (
        "Sub-task 4: Verify the computed side length of the hexagon by checking consistency with all given conditions: equilateral sides, parallel opposite sides, convexity, "
        "and the triangle side lengths formed by the extended lines. Provide a final answer for the hexagon's side length and confirm that no contradictions arise. "
        "If inconsistencies are found, revisit previous subtasks for refinement."
    )
    cot_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_4 = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3]
    subtask_desc4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_4",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_4,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content, answer1.content, thinking2.content, answer2.content, thinking3.content, answer3.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent_4(cot_inputs_4, cot_reflect_instruction_4, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_4.id}, verifying and refining hexagon side length, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    for i in range(N_max):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_4([taskInfo, thinking4, answer4], "Please review the answer above and criticize where it might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'.", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_4.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_4.extend([thinking4, answer4, feedback])
        thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent_4(cot_inputs_4, cot_reflect_instruction_4, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_4.id}, refining solution, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc4['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking4,
        "answer": answer4
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking4, answer4, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

The lines containing sides AB, CD, and EF are: Line AB passes through A(0,0) with direction vector (1,0). Line CD passes through C = AB + BC = s*(1 + cos θ, sin θ) with direction vector (cos φ, sin φ). Line EF passes through E = AB + BC + CD + DE = s*(cos θ + cos φ, sin θ + sin φ) with direction vector (-cos θ, -sin θ). We find the intersection points of these lines pairwise: 1) Intersection of lines AB and CD: Parametrize AB as (t,0), CD as C + u*(cos φ, sin φ). Setting y-coordinates equal: 0 = sin φ * u => u=0 or sin φ=0. Since sin φ ≠ 0 (to avoid degenerate hexagon), u=0. Then x-coordinates: t = s*(1 + cos θ). So intersection point P = (s*(1 + cos θ), 0). 2) Intersection of lines CD and EF: Parametrize CD as above, EF as E + v*(-cos θ, -sin θ). Set equal and solve for parameters. After algebraic manipulation, the intersection point Q is found. 3) Intersection of lines EF and AB: Parametrize EF and AB similarly and find intersection point R.     )
    N_sc_4 = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_4 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N_sc_4)]
    possible_answers_4 = []
    possible_thinkings_4 = []
    subtask_desc4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_4",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_4,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content, answer1.content, thinking2.content, answer2.content, thinking3.content, answer3.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N_sc_4):
        thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agents_4[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3], cot_sc_instruction_4, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_4[i].id}, solving system for hexagon side length, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
        possible_answers_4.append(answer4)
        possible_thinkings_4.append(thinking4)
    final_decision_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking4, answer4 = await final_decision_agent_4([taskInfo] + possible_answers_4 + possible_thinkings_4, "Sub-task 4: Synthesize and choose the most consistent and correct solution for the hexagon side length.", is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, synthesizing solution for hexagon side length, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc4['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking4,
        "answer": answer4
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflexion_instruction_5 = (
        "Sub-task 5: Critically verify the solution obtained in Subtask 4. "
        "Re-examine all derivations and assumptions, test alternative parameter values if applicable, and confirm that the computed hexagon side length s is consistent with all problem conditions. "
        "Perform numeric checks by substituting s, θ, and φ back into the expressions for triangle side lengths and hexagon side vectors. "
        "Identify any contradictions or unstated assumptions. Provide a final, justified answer for the hexagon side length. "
        "If inconsistencies arise, specify which subtasks require refinement and suggest corrective actions. "
        "This subtask should involve Reflexion and Debate collaboration to ensure thorough critical evaluation and consensus on the final solution."
    )
    cot_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_5 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_5 = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3, thinking4, answer4]
    subtask_desc5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": reflexion_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content, answer1.content, thinking2.content, answer2.content, thinking3.content, answer3.content, thinking4.content, answer4.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion | Debate"
    }
    thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agent_5(cot_inputs_5, reflexion_instruction_5, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_5.id}, verifying and refining hexagon side length, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_5):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_5([taskInfo, thinking5, answer5], "Please review the answer above and criticize where it might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'.", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_5.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_5.extend([thinking5, answer5, feedback])
        thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agent_5(cot_inputs_5, reflexion_instruction_5, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_5.id}, refining solution, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")
    subtask_desc5['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking5,
        "answer": answer5
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc5)
    print("Step 5: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking5, answer5, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

Q = L_CD ∩ L_EF\nSet parametric forms equal:\n(s/2 - u*s/2, s*sqrt(3)/2 - u*s*sqrt(3)/2) = (s - v*s/2, v*s*sqrt(3)/2)\nEquate x and y:\n s/2 - u*s/2 = s - v*s/2  (1)\n s*sqrt(3)/2 - u*s*sqrt(3)/2 = v*s*sqrt(3)/2  (2)\nDivide (1) by s/2:\n1 - u = 2 - v\n=> v = 1 + u\nDivide (2) by s*sqrt(3)/2:\n1 - u = v\nFrom above, v = 1 + u\nSo 1 - u = 1 + u\n=> -u = u\n=> u = 0\nThen v = 1 + 0 = 1\n\nSubstitute u=0 into L_CD:\nQ = (s/2, s*sqrt(3)/2)\n\n3. R = L_EF ∩ L_AB\nSet parametric forms equal:\n(t, 0) = (s - v*s/2, v*s*sqrt(3)/2)\nFrom y-coordinate:\n0 = v*s*sqrt(3)/2\n=> v=0\nFrom x-coordinate:\n t = s - 0 = s\n\nSo R = (s, 0)\n\nThus, the triangle formed by the intersections of lines AB, CD, and EF has vertices:\nP = (0,0), Q = (s/2, s*sqrt(3)/2), R = (s, 0)\n\nCompute side lengths:\n- PQ = distance between P and Q:\n= sqrt((s/2 - 0)^2 + (s*sqrt(3)/2 - 0)^2)\n= sqrt((s^2/4) + (3s^2/4)) = sqrt(s^2) = s\n\n- QR = distance between Q and R:\n= sqrt((s - s/2)^2 + (0 - s*sqrt(3)/2)^2)\n= sqrt((s/2)^2 + (-s*sqrt(3)/2)^2)\n= sqrt(s^2/4 + 3s^2/4) = sqrt(s^2) = s\n\n- RP = distance between R and P:\n= sqrt((s - 0)^2 + (0 - 0)^2) = s\n\nTherefore, triangle PQR is equilateral with side length s.\n\nGiven the problem states the triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF has side lengths 200, 240, and 300, which are not equal, this contradicts the above result. R = L_EF ∩ L_AB\nSet parametric forms equal:\n(t, 0) = (s - v*s/2, v*s*sqrt(3)/2)\nFrom y-coordinate:\n0 = v*s*sqrt(3)/2\n=> v=0\nFrom x-coordinate:\n t = s - 0 = s\n\nSo R = (s, 0)\n\nThus, the triangle formed by the intersections of lines AB, CD, and EF has vertices:\nP = (0,0), Q = (s/2, s*sqrt(3)/2), R = (s, 0)\n\nCompute side lengths:\n- PQ = distance between P and Q:\n= sqrt((s/2 - 0)^2 + (s*sqrt(3)/2 - 0)^2)\n= sqrt((s^2/4) + (3s^2/4)) = sqrt(s^2) = s\n\n- QR = distance between Q and R:\n= sqrt((s - s/2)^2 + (0 - s*sqrt(3)/2)^2)\n= sqrt((s/2)^2 + (-s*sqrt(3)/2)^2)\n= sqrt(s^2/4 + 3s^2/4) = sqrt(s^2) = s\n\n- RP = distance between R and P:\n= sqrt((s - 0)^2 + (0 - 0)^2) = s\n\nTherefore, triangle PQR is equilateral with side length s.\n\nGiven the problem states the triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF has side lengths 200, 240, and 300, which are not equal, this contradicts the above result. This suggests the hexagon is not regular but equilateral with opposite sides parallel, and the directions θ and φ are not 120° and 240° but different.\n\nHence, the initial assumption θ=120°, φ=240° is not valid for the problem\'s triangle side lengths.\n\nTo generalize, let’s define:\n- AB along x-axis: vector AB = s*(1,0)\n- BC at angle θ: vector BC = s*(cos θ, sin θ)\n- CD at angle φ: vector CD = s*(cos φ, sin φ)\n\nOpposite sides parallel imply:\n- DE parallel to AB => DE = s*(1,0)\n- EF parallel to BC => EF = s*(cos θ, sin θ)\n- FA parallel to CD => FA = s*(cos φ, sin φ)\n\nClosure condition:\nAB + BC + CD + DE + EF + FA = 0\n=> s*(1,0) + s*(cos θ, sin θ) + s*(cos φ, sin φ) + s*(1,0) + s*(cos θ, sin θ) + s*(cos φ, sin φ) = 0\n=> s*[2 + 2 cos θ + 2 cos φ, 2 sin θ + 2 sin φ] = 0\nDivide by 2s:\n[1 + cos θ + cos φ, sin θ + sin φ] = 0\n\nFrom this:\n1 + cos θ + cos φ = 0\nsin θ + sin φ = 0\n\nFrom sin θ + sin φ = 0 => sin φ = - sin θ\nFrom 1 + cos θ + cos φ = 0 => cos φ = -1 - cos θ\n\nUsing cos^2 φ + sin^2 φ = 1:\n(-1 - cos θ)^2 + (- sin θ)^2 = 1\n=> (1 + 2 cos θ + cos^2 θ) + sin^2 θ = 1\n=> 1 + 2 cos θ + 1 = 1\n=> 2 + 2 cos θ = 1\n=> cos θ = -1/2\n\nThis leads back to θ=120°, φ=240°, which contradicts the triangle side lengths given.\n\nTherefore, the problem\'s triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF is not the triangle formed by the intersection points of the lines containing these sides but rather the triangle formed by the lines themselves, i.e., the triangle formed by the three lines AB, CD, and EF intersecting pairwise at points P, Q, R.\n\nTo find the side lengths of triangle PQR formed by the intersection points of lines AB, CD, and EF, we proceed as follows:\n\nLines:\n- AB: passes through A(0,0), direction vector d_AB = (1,0)\n- CD: passes through C = AB + BC + CD = s*(1 + cos θ + cos φ, 0 + sin θ + sin φ)\n- EF: passes through E = AB + BC + CD + DE + EF = s*(2 + cos θ, sin θ)\n\nDirection vectors:\n- AB: (1,0)\n- CD: (cos φ, sin φ)\n- EF: (cos θ, sin θ)\n\nParametric equations:\n- AB: x = t, y = 0\n- CD: x = x_C + u*cos φ, y = y_C + u*sin φ\n- EF: x = x_E + v*cos θ, y = y_E + v*sin θ\n\nFind intersections:\n- P = AB ∩ CD\nSet y=0 = y_C + u*sin φ => u = - y_C / sin φ\nThen x = t = x_C + u*cos φ\n- Q = CD ∩ EF\nSolve system:\nx_C + u*cos φ = x_E + v*cos θ\ny_C + u*sin φ = y_E + v*sin θ\n- R = EF ∩ AB\nSet y=0 = y_E + v*sin θ => v = - y_E / sin θ\nThen x = t = x_E + v*cos θ\n\nExpress P, Q, R in terms of s, θ, φ, then compute distances PQ, QR, RP symbolically.\n\nThis process yields expressions for the triangle side lengths in terms of s, θ, and φ.\n\nGiven the triangle side lengths 200, 240, and 300, one can solve for s.\n\nIn summary, the parametric equations of lines AB, CD, and EF are:\n- AB: (x,y) = (t, 0)\n- CD: (x,y) = (s*(1 + cos θ + cos φ), s*(sin θ + sin φ)) + u*(cos φ, sin φ)\n- EF: (x,y) = (s*(2 + cos θ), s*sin θ) + v*(cos θ, sin θ)\n\nThe intersection points P, Q, R are:\n- P = AB ∩ CD\n- Q = CD ∩ EF\n- R = EF ∩ AB\n\nTheir coordinates and the side lengths of triangle PQR can be explicitly expressed in terms of s, θ, and φ by solving the above equations.\n\nThis completes the derivation of the parametric equations, intersection points, and symbolic side lengths of triangle PQR in terms of the hexagon side length s and parameters θ and φ.\n\n### answer by Chain-of-Thought Agent xeeY:\nLines containing sides AB, CD, and EF are:\n- AB: passes through A(0,0) with direction vector (1,0), parametric form: (x,y) = (t, 0)\n- CD: passes through C = s*(1 + cos θ + cos φ, sin θ + sin φ) with direction vector (cos φ, sin φ), parametric form: (x,y) = (s*(1 + cos θ + cos φ), s*(sin θ + sin φ)) + u*(cos φ, sin φ)\n- EF: passes through E = s*(2 + cos θ, sin θ) with direction vector (cos θ, sin θ), parametric form: (x,y) = (s*(2 + cos θ), s*sin θ) + v*(cos θ, sin θ)\n\nThe intersection points forming triangle PQR are:\n- P = AB ∩ CD: solve y=0 = s*(sin θ + sin φ) + u*sin φ => u = -
